text: "33\nQ. 75. Whom did God from eternity predestinate, or\nelect to everlasting life?\nA. All those who, accepting his gracious call, re-\npent and believe in the Lord Jesus Christ, and remain\nfaithful to the end.\nDECREES AND PROVIDENCE OF GOD.\nQ. 76. Why did God determine to condemn others to\neternal punishment?\nA. Because they resisted the Holy Spirit, rejected\nthe offers of mercy, and died in their sins.\nQ. 77. What duties does the doctrine of divine provi-\ndence require of us?\nA. That we should habitually recognize the fatherly\nhand of God in all things, and pray for his guidance\nand protection, as well as be patient in adversity and\nhumbly thankful in prosperity.\nmight feel after him, and find him, though he be not far\nfrom every one of us: for in him we live, and move, and\nhave our being; as certain also of your own poets have\nsaid, For we are also his offspring. Heb. i. 3. Jer. v. 24.\nActs xiv. 17: Nevertheless he left not himself without\nwitness, in that he did good, and gave us rain from hea-\nven, and fruitful seasons, filling our hearts with food and\ngladness. John ix. 3. Prov. xxii. 2. Job i. 21. Matt.\nx. 29, 30: Are not two sparrows sold for a farthing? and\none of them shall not fall on the ground without your\nFather. But the very hairs of your head are all num-\nbered. MONTERINGAR SITE\nQ. 75. Rom. viii. 29: For whom he did foreknow, he\nalso did predestinate to be conformed to the image of his\nSon, that he might be the firstborn among many brethren.\n1 Pet. i. 2: Elect according to the foreknowledge of God\nthe Father, through sanctification of the Spirit, unto obe-\ndience and sprinkling of the blood of Jesus Christ: Grace\nunto you, and peace, be multiplied.\nQ. 76. Mark xvi. 16: He that believeth and is bap-\ntized shall be saved; but he that believeth not shall be\ndamned. Rom. viii. 29.\nQ. 77. Deut. viii. 1: When thou hast eaten and art\nfull, then thou shalt bless the LORD thy God for the good"
